 The Prime Minister has assured all the news channels that the final decision will be taken only after discussions with everyone
 gauratlab he ki is bill ke virodh main saare media vaale ekajute ho gaye hai
 At the same time, politics is also being done on this issue
 kai raajnneetik dalon ne media par pabandi lagane kaa virodh kiya he
 The leaders of the Samajwadi Party, already angry with the Congress, are not happy with the idea of censorship on the media
 party mahasachiv amar singh ke mutabik isse to abhivyakti kii aazaadee khatm ho jaaegi, or is masale ko lekar wo pradhanmantri se milane bhi jaayenge
 According to BJP President Rajnath Singh, he is against any kind of ban on media
 bijepi adhyaksh kaa kahana he ki sarkaar koi bhi faisla karne se pehle sabhi raajnneetik dalon se baatcheet kare
 JDU president Sharad Yadav is also against tying the media to any realm

 seetaram yechuri ne kaha he ki media ke liye independent regulatory maikenism honi chahie

 bachaler of commers (B
 Com): If you want to do three years graduation in commerce after 12th, then bcom is a good option
 is degree kii madad se aap acounting finans, oparations, texeshan or duusare kai fields main apana kariyar bana sakate hai

 2
 bachaler of commers (onors):akasar students bachaler of commers (onors) or bachaler of commers main antar nahin kar pate

 students ko in vishyon ke alaava ek vishay main speshligeshan bhi karaayaa jaataa he

 bachaler of commers main subjects onors kii tulana main kam detail main padhaaye jate hai
 3
 bikom- accounting and finans (B
 com-accts and Finance): Bachelor of Commerce in Accounting and Finance is a three-year degree program conducted after 12th standard
 is course ke baad acounts or finans main kariyar ke maukey kaaphi hote hai
 In the initial days one can work as a trainee accountant
 is program main acounts, finans, texeshan ke kareeb 39 vishay padhaaye jate hai
 This degree program focuses more on financial knowledge
 4
 bcom-banking and Insurance: Bachelor of Commerce (banking and Insurance) is both an academic and professional degree
 is program main acounting, banking, insurance lau, banking lau or insurance risk cover kii jaankaree di jaati he
 In this degree, a systematic study of topics and topics covered in the banking and insurance industry is conducted
 is course main 38 vishay hote hai
 Apart from this, there are 2 projects related to banking and insurance
 is course ko karne ke baad students emcom, emb, sieciae jaise hair ajukeshan vaale corcej kar sakate hai
 Not only this, it can also be applied for jobs in the field of auditing, accountancy, banking, finance in the government and private sector
 5
 Cost and Work Accountant (CWA): Cost Accountancy is a course similar to CA
 da institute of cost and works acountint of india cost acountency kaa course karaata he
 Even after 12th, students can take ICWA course
 iske liye 12veen paas students ko pehle foundation course karnaa hota he
 After completing the course, students get a chance to work on the cost accountant and related posts
 iske liye da institut of cost and work acountents of india main aavedan karnaa hota he
 Entrance exam takes place in June and December for admission
 foundation course ke baad intermediat course karnaa hota he or phir sie kii tarah hi final exam dekar course puraa hota he
 6
 bikom- finantial markets:
 Information about finance, investments, stock market, capital, mutual funds are given in Bachelor of Commerce in Financial Markets
 is program main 6 semester hote hai or kul 41 vishyon kii padhai kii jaati he
 After obtaining this degree, one can get a job as a Trainee Associate, Finance Officer, Finance Controller, Finance Planner, Risk Management, Money Market Dealer Insurance Manager
 7
 Chartered Accountant: The Institute of Chartered Accountants of India (ICAI) offers a Chartered Accountant course
 sie main kariyar banane ke liye isaki shuruyaat kaaman prophysiency test (CPT) se hoti he, jise paas karne ke baad hi chaatr apane lakshya ke pehle padaav ko paar kar duusare padaav par pahunch saktaa he

 manyata praapt board se cormas stream main 12veen paas karne ke baad koi bhi students sie main kariyar bana sakate hai

 lekin sie course kii lambii avadhi ke kaaran sie kii shuruyaat kaa sahi samay 12veen paas karne ke baad kaa hi hota he

 8

 iske teen charan hai- foundation (aath maheene), agjicutive or profeshnal

 bibie:haalanki kisi bhi stream se 12veen karne vaale student bibie kar sakate hai, lekin commers students ke bich yah course khaasaa lokipriy he

 *** srilanka or mehmaan bangladesh kii tiimon ke bich galle antarrashtriya stadium main khelaa gaya shrunkhlaa kaa pehla test match mangalvaar ko benatija samaapt ho gaya
 On the final day of the match, Sri Lanka declared their second innings for 335 runs by losing four wickets and aiming for 268 runs to win in front of Bangladesh, in response to which Bangladesh lost 70 runs by losing one wicket in 22 overs till four in the evening
 Were made iske baad koi nateeja na nikalataa dekh captainon ne aapasi sahmati se match khatm karne kaa faisla kiya
 Zahurul Islam 41 and Mohammad Ashraful 22 were frozen at the crease till the match was announced
 do maichon kii shrunkhlaa ke is pehle mukaable main bangladesh ke captain mushafikur rahim (200) ko unki shandaar pari ke liye 'main of da match' ke khitaab se nawaja gaya
 However, this match has taken a total of eight centuries, which is a record
 isse pehle, westeindies or dakshin africa ke bich antiga main varsh 2005 main khele gaye test match main aath shatak lage the
 The Sri Lankan batsmen also performed brilliantly in the second innings in the match
 kumaar sangakaara (105) ne duusari pari main bhi shandaar shatak lagaaya, jabaki tillakaratne dilashaan (126) ne bhi is pari main shatkeey score banaaya
 Both these batsmen shared 213 runs for the second wicket
 mejabaan team kii ore se kithruvan vinthaj ne bhi naabad 58 ran banaae
 Sri Lanka declared their second innings at 335 for four wickets
 bangladesh kii ore se sabase zyada teen wicket mahamudullah ko mili
 Earlier, the fourth day of the match was named after Bangladesh captain Mushfiqur Rahim
 mushafikur bangladesh ke liye test cricket main pehla doharaa shatak lagane vaale ballebaaj bane
 Not only this, he also got the record for playing the biggest private innings for Bangladesh
 unhone 200 ranon kii pari ke dauraan 321 genden khelin or 22 chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Before this Test, the record for the biggest innings for Bangladesh was in the name of Mohammad Ashraful, who scored an innings of 158 runs against India, but during this Test, Ashraful broke his record
 ashraful ne 190 ran banaae or vah mahaj 10 ran se apana pehla doharaa shatak lagane se chook gaye
 Ashraful and Mushfiqur shared a partnership of 267 runs for the fifth wicket and set a record
 yah bangladesh ke liye kisi bhi wicket ke liye sabase badi saajhedaari he
 The comments bangladesh kii ore se nasir hossain ne bhi shatak lagaaya tha
 Bangladesh had scored 638 runs in the first innings, while Sri Lanka declared their first innings for 570 runs for four wickets
 is tarah se bangladesh ko srilanka kii pehali pari ke mukaable 68 ranon kii badhat hasil hui thi
 For Sri Lanka, Nuwan Kulasekara, Dilshan, Rangana Herath and Shaminda Eranga took two wickets each
 shrunkhlaa kaa aglaa or aakhri test match colombo ke premdasa stadium main 16 march se khelaa jayega
 In this first match of the two-match series, Bangladesh captain Mushfiqur Rahim (200) was awarded the title of 'man of the Match' for his brilliant innings
 vaise is match main kul aath shatak lage hai, jo ek record he
 Earlier, the Test match played in the year 2005 in Antiga between West Indies and South Africa had eight centuries
 match main srilanka ke ballebaajon ne duusari pari main bhi shandaar pradarshan kiya
 Kumar Sangakkara (105) also scored a brilliant century in the second innings, while Tillakaratne Dilshan (126) also scored a century in this innings
 in donon ballebaajon ne duusare wicket ke liye 213 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Kithruvan Vinthaj also scored an unbeaten 58 from the hosts
 srilanka ne apni duusari pari chaar wicket par 335 ranon par ghoshit kii
 Mahmudullah got the most three wickets from Bangladesh
 isse pehle, match kaa chauthaa din bangladesh ke captain mushafikur rahim ke naam rahaa tha
 Mushfiqur became the batsman to score the first double century in Test cricket for Bangladesh
 yahi nahin, unke naam bangladesh ke liye sabase badi nijee pari khelnaa kaa bhi record darj ho gaya
 He played 321 balls during the innings of 200 runs and hit 22 fours and a six
 is test se pehle bangladesh ke liye sabase badi pari khilne kaa record mohammad ashraful ke naam tha, jinhone bharat ke khilaaf 158 ranon kaa pari kheli thi, lekin isi test ke dauraan ashraful ne apana record tod diya
 Ashraful scored 190 runs and missed his first double century by just 10 runs
 ashraful or mushafikur ne paanchaven wicket ke liye 267 ranon kii saajhedaari nibhaai thi or ek record kaayam kiya
 This is the biggest partnership for any wicket for Bangladesh
 tippaniyan Nasir Hussain also scored a century from Bangladesh
 bangladesh ne pehali pari main 638 ran banaae the, jabaki srilanka ne apni pehali pari chaar wicket par 570 ranon par ghoshit kii thi

 srilanka kii ore se nuwan kulshekhara, dilashaan, rangana herath or shaminda irangaa ne do-do wicket hasil kiye
